					OR = {

							ruling_only = yes

						}

		}

				add_idea = proper_science_base
			}
		}

		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = SLC_hydra_timer
			days = 365
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.majors
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
				add_ideas = SLC_reactionary_hydra_idea
			}
		}
	}
}
